     <h1>
      Welcome to Godchecker
     </h1>
     <h2>
      We have more Gods than you can shake a stick at.
     </h2>
     <div class="dodbox hover-panel GC2" id="pullout-box">
      <a href="http://www.godchecker.com/pantheon/norse-mythology.php?deity=GULVEIG">
       <h1>
        Deity of the day
       </h1>
       <h2>
        GULVEIG
       </h2>
       <h3>
        Goddess of Greed from Norse mythology
       </h3>
       <p>
        Gold-obsessed Giantess.
       </p>
      </a>
     </div>
     <p>
      Our legendary mythology encyclopedia now includes nearly four thousand weird and wonderful
      <strong>
       Gods, Supreme Beings, Demons, Spirits
      </strong>
      and
      <strong>
       Fabulous Beasts
      </strong>
      from all over the world. Explore ancient legends and folklore, and discover Gods of everything from Fertility to Fluff with Godchecker...
     </p>
     <noscript>
      <p>
       Browse the pantheons of mythology and meet weird and wonderful Gods from around the world. We're adding new information all the time as our mythology database expands to infinite size. All Gods and Goddesses are detailed, many with alternative names, pronunciation, research, speculation and images.
      </p>
     </noscript>

     <h2>
      THE HOLY HIT PARADE
     </h2>
     <p>
      Who's the most popular God? Our patent GodRank™ technology has the answer.
      <a href="top-gods/index.php?popular-gods">
       See the Top Ten Gods here
      </a>
      .
     </p>
     <p>
      <b>
       Confused? Consult the Godchecker
       <a href="oracle/index.php">
        FAQ
       </a>
       .
      </b>
     </p>
     <p>
      For maximum blessings, follow the Gods on
      <b>
       Twitter
      </b>
      <a href="http://twitter.com/Godchecker" onclick="openWin(this);return false">
       @Godchecker
      </a>
      and get daily deities on
      <b>
       Facebook
      </b>
      at the official
      <a href="http://www.facebook.com/Godchecker" onclick="openWin(this);return false">
       Godchecker HQ
      </a>
      page.
     </p>
     <p>
      <span class="txt-notes">
       Godchecker is 100% non-denominational. Our Holy Database aims to cover all Gods of mythology, literature and legend. All Gods are welcome, whether Greek, Roman, Egyptian, or of No Fixed Abode. Polytheism is much more fun than monotonous monotheism. Terry Pratchett fans, Tolkien aficionados, Douglas Adams devotees, Lovecraft lovers and Harry Potter nuts will love our selection of Goddities.
      </span>
     </p>
     <p>
      All our Gods are certified genuine.
     </p>

      This site is blessed by the Holy Snail™
